<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:класть.html>класть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складывать.html>скла́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skládyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сложить.html>сложи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lay together, to put together, to pile up, to heap, to stack</li>
<li>to pack up</li>
<li>to add, to sum up</li>
<li>to make, to assemble, to put together</li>
<li><i>song, rhyme</i> to compose, to make up</li>
<li>to fold</li>
<li>to take off, to put down</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:складываться.html>скла́дываться</a> (4393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складывать.html>скла́дывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складываться.html>скла́дываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skládyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сложиться.html>сложи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to club together (with), to pool (with), to pool one's money / resources</li>
<li>to (be) form(ed), to develop, to turn out, to take shape; to arise <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a situation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складывать.html>скла́дывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>скла́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ды<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:склеить.html>скле́ить</a> (13752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеить.html>кле́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kléitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склеить.html>скле́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skléitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеить.html>кле́ить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склеивать.html>скле́ивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to glue together, to paste together, to stick together</li>
<li>to mend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбитый.html>разби́тую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дружба.html>дру́жбу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:склеить.html>скле́ишь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razbítuju drúžbu ne <b>skléišʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a broken friendship can't be mended</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонить.html>склони́ть</a> (5399)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клонить.html>клони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонить.html>склони́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sklonítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонять.html>склоня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bend, to incline, to decline</li>
<li>to convince someone to do something</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decline a noun or adjective</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:склониться.html>склони́ться</a> (4196)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонить.html>склони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sklonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склониться.html>склони́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sklonítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to incline, to bend, to stoop</li>
<li>to be inclined (to)</li>
<li>to yield (to) (to give up under pressure)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонить.html>склони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sklonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***склонность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонность.html>скло́нность</a> (6750)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонный.html>скло́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sklónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонность.html>скло́нность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sklónnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонность.html>скло́нности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонность.html>скло́нности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонность.html>скло́нностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>propensity, proclivity</li>
<li>tendency, inclination, disposition</li>
<li>leaning, penchant</li>
<li>predilection</li>
<li>taste</li>
<li>addiction</li>
<li>bent</li>
<li>aptitude</li>
<li>predisposition</li>
<li>appetite</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонять.html>склоня́ть</a> (16941)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонять.html>склоня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sklonjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонить.html>склони́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">просклоня́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bend, to incline, to decline
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонить.html>склони́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sklonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to convince someone to do something
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонить.html>склони́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sklonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decline a noun or adjective
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">просклоня́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prosklonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонять.html>склоня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sklonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sklonjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склониться.html>склони́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to incline, to bend, to stoop</li>
<li>to be inclined (to)</li>
<li>to yield (to) (to give up under pressure)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склонять.html>склоня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sklonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:склянка.html>скля́нка</a> (14657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склянка.html>скля́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skljánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склянка.html>скля́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склянка.html>скля́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склянка.html>скля́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vial, flask, bottle, glass</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">naval</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bell, half an hour
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>пробило</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шесть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:склянка.html>скля́нок</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">probilo šestʹ <b>skljánok</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">six bells went</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">naval<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(plural)</i> watch glass, hourglass</li></ol>

***скобка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скобка.html>ско́бка</a> (11214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скоба.html>скоба́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skobá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скобка.html>ско́бка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skóbka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скобка.html>ско́бки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скобка.html>ско́бки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скобка.html>ско́бок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">typography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> parenthesis, bracket

***сковать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́ть</a> (12475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковать.html>кова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forge, to hammer out</li>
<li>to forge together</li>
<li>to chain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hold, to fix
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огнём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skovátʹ</b> ognjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pin (down) by fire</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratevly<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with ice</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lock, to beset
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́з</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:лед.html>лёд</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>ре́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">moróz/ljod <b>skovál</b> réku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the river is frozen over; the river is icebound</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fetter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>страх</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">strax <b>skovál</b> mne dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I was overcome/seized with fear</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
